article=article)\n\n\n@app.route('/bookmarks', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef bookmarks():\n    bookmarks = read_bookmarks()\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        # Remove bookmark\n        for key in request.form.keys():\n            if key.startswith('remove-bookmark-button-'):\n                bookmark_id = key.replace('remove-bookmark-button-', '')\n                bookmarks = [b for b in bookmarks if b['bookmark_id'] != bookmark_id]\n                write_bookmarks(bookmarks)\n                return redirect(url_for('bookmarks'))\n            elif key.startswith('read-bookmark-button-'):\n                bookmark_id = key.replace('read-bookmark-button-', '')\n                bookmark = next((b for b in bookmarks if b['bookmark_id'] == bookmark_id), None)\n                if bookmark:\n                    return redirect(url_for('article_details', article_id=bookmark['article_id']))\n    return render_template('bookmarks.html', bookmarks=bookmarks)\n\n\n@app.route('/comments', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef comments():\n    comments = read_comments()\n    articles = read_articles()\n    filter_article = request.args.get('filter-by-article', '')\n\n    filtered_comments = comments\n    if filter_article:\n        filtered_comments = [c for c in comments if c['article_title'] == filter_article]\n\n    categories = [c['category_name'] for c in read_categories()]\n    article_titles = [a['title'] for a in articles]\n\n    return render_template('comments.html', comments=filtered_comments, articles=article_titles, selected_article=filter_article)\n\n\n@app.route('/write-comment', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef write_comment():\n    articles = read_articles()\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        article_id = request.form.get('select-article')\n        commenter_name = request.form.get('commenter-name', '').strip()\n        comment_text = request.form.get('comment-text', '').strip()\n        if not (article_id and commenter_name and comment_text):\n            error = 'Please fill in all fields.'\n            return render_template('write_comment.html', articles=articles, error=error)\n\n        article = next((a for a in articles if a['article_id'] == article_id), None)\n        if not article:\n            error = 'Selected article not found.'\n            return render_template('write_comment.html', articles=articles, error=error)\n\n        comments = read_comments()\n        comment_id = str(len(comments) + 1)\n        comment_date = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')\n        new_comment = {\n            'comment_id': comment_id,\n            'article_id': article_id,\n            'article_title': article['title'],\n            'commenter_name': commenter_name,\n            'comment_text': comment_text,\n            'comment_date': comment_date\n        }\n        write_comment(new_comment)\n        return redirect(url_for('comments'))\n    return render_template('write_comment.html', articles=articles)\n\n\n@app.route('/trending', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef trending():\n    trending = read_trending()\n    time_period = request.args.get('time-period-filter', 'This Week')\n    filtered_trending = [t for t in trending if t['period'] == time_period]\n\n    # Sort by view_count descending\n    filtered_trending.sort(key=lambda x: x['view_count'], reverse=True)\n\n    return render_template('trending.html', trending_list=filtered_trending, time_period=time_period)\n\n\n@app.route('/category/<category_name>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef category(category_name):\n    articles = read_articles()\n    category_articles = [a for a in articles if a['category'] == category_name]\n\n    sort_by = None\n    reverse = False\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        sort_by = request.form.get('sort-by', '')\n        if sort_by == 'date':\n            # Toggle sorting by date\n            # We'll check a param to toggle ascending/descending\n            toggle = request.form.get('toggle', 'asc')\n            reverse = (toggle == 'desc')\n            category_articles.sort(key=lambda x: x['date'], reverse=reverse)\n        elif sort_by == 'popularity':\n            category_articles.sort(key=lambda x: x['views'], reverse=True)\n\n    return render_template('category.html', category_name=category_name, category_articles=category_articles)\n\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    app.run(debug=True)\n\n\n=== Latest Overview\nThis document specifies the complete design of the NewsPortal Flask web app, covering all 9 pages with detailed element IDs, navigation flow starting from Dashboard, and local text file data storage formats.\n\n---\n\n## 2. Flask Page Templates and UI Elements\n\n### 2.1 Dashboard Page\n- **Route:** `/dashboard` (Starting page)\n- **Page Title:** `News Portal`\n- **Container Div:** `id=\"dashboard-page\"`\n- **UI Elements:**\n  - `div` with `id=\"featured-articles\"` - displays recommended featured articles\n  - `button` with `id=\"browse-articles-button\"` - navigates to Article Catalog page\n  - `button` with `id=\"view-bookmarks-button\"` - navigates to Bookmarks page\n  - `button` with `id=\"trending-articles-button\"` - navigates to Trending Articles page\n\n### 2.2 Article Catalog Page\n- **Route:** `/catalog`\n- **Page Title:** `Article Catalog`\n- **Container Div:** `id=\"catalog-page\"`\n- **UI Elements:**\n  - `input` (text) with `id=\"search-input\"` - to search articles by title, author, or keywords\n  - `select` dropdown with `id=\"category-filter\"` - categories filter (Technology, Sports, Business, Health, Entertainment, etc.)\n  - `div` with `id=\"articles-grid\"` - grid layout for article cards\n  - For each article card:\n     - `button` with `id=\"view-article-button-{article_id}\"` - to view article details\n\n### 2.3 Article Details Page\n- **Route:** `/article/<article_id>`\n- **Page Title:** `Article Details`\n- **Container Div:** `id=\"article-details-page\"`\n- **UI Elements:**\n  - `h1` with `id=\"article-title\"` - article title\n  - `div` with `id=\"article-author\"` - article author\n  - `div` with `id=\"article-date\"` - publication date\n  - `button` with `id=\"bookmark-button\"` - to bookmark this article\n  - `div` with `id=\"article-content\"` - full article content\n\n### 2.4 Bookmarks Page\n- **Route:** `/bookmarks`\n- **Page Title:** `My Bookmarks`\n- **Container Div:** `id=\"bookmarks-page\"`\n- **UI Elements:**\n  - `div` with `id=\"bookmarks-list\"` - list showing bookmarked articles with title and date\n  - For each bookmark:\n    - `button` with `id=\"remove-bookmark-button-{bookmark_id}\"` - remove bookmark\n    - `button` with `id=\"read-bookmark-button-{bookmark_id}\"` - read bookmarked article\n  - `button` with `id=\"back-to-dashboard\"` - navigate back to Dashboard\n\n### 2.5 Comments Page\n- **Route:** `/comments`\n- **Page Title:** `Article Comments`\n- **Container Div:** `id=\"comments-page\"`\n- **UI Elements:**\n  - `div` with `id=\"comments-list\"` - list of all comments with article title, commenter name, and comment text\n  - `button` with `id=\"write-comment-button\"` - navigate to Write Comment page\n  - `select` dropdown with `id=\"filter-by-article\"` - filter comments by article\n  - `button` with `id=\"back-to-dashboard\"` - navigate back to Dashboard\n\n### 2.6 Write Comment Page\n- **Route:** `/write-comment`\n- **Page Title:** `Write a Comment`\n- **Container Div:** `id=\"write-comment-page\"`\n- **UI Elements:**\n  - `select` dropdown with `id=\"select-article\"` - select article to comment on\n  - `input` (text) with `id=\"commenter-name\"` - enter commenter name\n  - `textarea` with `id=\"comment-text\"` - enter comment\n  - `button` with `id=\"submit-comment-button\"` - submit comment\n\n### 2.7 Trending Articles Page\n- **Route:** `/trending`\n- **Page Title:** `Trending Articles`\n- **Container Div:** `id=\"trending-page\"`\n- **UI Elements:**\n  - `div` with `id=\"trending-list\"` - ranked trending articles showing rank, title, category, view count\n  - `select` dropdown with `id=\"time-period-filter\"` - filter by time period (Today, This Week, This Month)\n  - For each trending article:\n    - `button` with `id=\"view-article-button-{article_id}\"` - view article details\n  - `button` with `id=\"back-to-dashboard\"` - navigate back to Dashboard\n\n### 2.8 Category Page\n- **Route:** `/category/<category_name>`\n- **Page Title:** `Category Articles`\n- **Container Div:** `id=\"category-page\"`\n- **UI Elements:**\n  - `h1` with `id=\"category-title\"` - name of the category\n  - `div` with `id=\"category-articles\"` - list of articles in that category\n  - `button` with `id=\"sort-by-date\"` - sort articles by date\n  - `button` with `id=\"sort-by-popularity\"` - sort articles by popularity\n  - `button` with `id=\"back-to-dashboard\"` - navigate back to Dashboard\n\n### 2.9 Search Results Page\n- **Route:** `/search-results`\n- **Page Title:** `Search Results`\n- **Container Div:** `id=\"search-results-page\"`\n- **UI Elements:**\n  - `div` with `id=\"search-query-display\"` - display the executed search query\n  - `div` with `id=\"results-list\"` - list of articles matching the search\n  - `div` with `id=\"no-results-message\"` - message when no results found\n  - `button` with `id=\"back-to-dashboard\"` - navigate back to Dashboard\n\n---\n\n## 3. Navigation Flow\n\n- Application default start page: `/dashboard` (Dashboard Page)\n\n- From Dashboard:\n  - `browse-articles-button` → `/catalog`\n  - `view-bookmarks-button` → `/bookmarks`\n  - `trending-articles-button` → `/trending`\n\n- From Article Catalog:\n  - `view-article-button-{article_id}` → `/article/{article_id}`\n  - Filter by category uses `/category/{category_name}` page\n  - Search submits query and navigates to `/search-results`\n  - No explicit back button (assumed via browser or nav bar)\n\n- From Article Details:\n  - `bookmark-button` adds bookmark\n  - Navigation back via browser or site nav (no explicit back button required)\n\n- From Bookmarks:\n  - `remove-bookmark-button-{bookmark_id}` removes the bookmark\n  - `read-bookmark-button-{bookmark_id}` navigates to `/article/{article_id}`\n  - `back-to-dashboard` → `/dashboard`\n\n- From Comments:\n  - `write-comment-button` → `/write-comment`\n  - `filter-by-article` updates displayed comments\n  - `back-to-dashboard` → `/dashboard`\n\n- From Write Comment:\n  - `submit-comment-button` submits new comment and redirects to `/comments`\n\n- From Trending:\n  - `view-article-button-{article_id}` → `/article/{article_id}`\n  - `time-period-filter` changes trending articles display\n  - `back-to-dashboard` → `/dashboard`\n\n- From Category:\n  - `sort-by-date` sorts articles ascending/descending by date\n  - `sort-by-popularity` sorts by views\n  - `back-to-dashboard` → `/dashboard`\n\n- From Search Results:\n  - `back-to-dashboard` → `/dashboard`\n\n---\n\n## 4. Local Text File Data Storage Formats and Usage\n\nAll data is stored in the `data/` directory in UTF-8 encoded text files.\n\n### 4.1 Articles Data (`articles.txt`)\n- **File Path:** `data/articles.txt`\n- **Format:** \n  ```\n  article_id|title|author|category|content|date|views\n  ```\n- **Example:**\n  ```\n  1|Breaking: New Technology Breakthrough|John Smith|Technology|Revolutionary advancement in quantum computing announced today|2025-01-20|5432\n  2|Sports: Championship Victory|Sarah Johnson|Sports|Team wins the national championship with a thrilling final match|2025-01-19|3210\n  3|Business: Market Trends Analysis|Michael Chen|Business|Expert analysis of current market conditions and forecasts|2025-01-18|2891\n  ```\n- **Usage:** Load at app start or on-demand to display articles; update views on article reads.\n\n### 4.2 Categories Data (`categories.txt`)\n- **File Path:** `data/categories.txt`\n- **Format:** \n  ```\n  category_id|category_name|description\n  ```\n- **Example:**\n  ```\n  1|Technology|Latest tech news and innovations\n  2|Sports|Sports news and event coverage\n  3|Business|Business and finance news\n  ```\n- **Usage:** Populate category filters and category page displays.\n\n### 4.3 Bookmarks Data (`bookmarks.txt`)\n- **File Path:** `data/bookmarks.txt`\n- **Format:**\n  ```\n  bookmark_id|article_id|article_title|bookmarked_date\n  ```\n- **Example:**\n  ```\n  1|1|Breaking: New Technology Breakthrough|2025-01-20\n  2|3|Business: Market Trends Analysis|2025-01-18\n  ```\n- **Usage:** Read to show user bookmarks; add/remove bookmarks updates this file.\n\n### 4.4 Comments Data (`comments.txt`)\n- **File Path:** `data/comments.txt`\n- **Format:**\n  ```\n  comment_id|article_id|article_title|commenter_name|comment_text|comment_date\n  ```\n- **Example:**\n  ```\n  1|1|Breaking: New Technology Breakthrough|Alice Davis|Fascinating development!|2025-01-20\n  2|2|Sports: Championship Victory|Robert Wilson|Amazing performance by the team!|2025-01-19\n  ```\n- **Usage:** Read to display comments; append on new comment submission.\n\n### 4.5 Trending Data (`trending.txt`)\n- **File Path:** `data/trending.txt`\n- **Format:**\n  ```\n  article_id|article_title|category|view_count|period\n  ```\n- **Example:**\n  ```\n  1|Breaking: New Technology Breakthrough|Technology|5432|This Week\n  2|Sports: Championship Victory|Sports|3210|This Week\n  3|Business: Market Trends Analysis|Business|2891|This Month\n  ```\n- **Usage:** Used for Trending page display filtered by time period.\n\n---\n\n## 5. Summary\nThis design specification fully encompasses the required UI elements with exact IDs for all pages, the navigation flow starting from the Dashboard page, and the precise format and usage of all text file-based data stores as specified in the requirements.\n\nThis spec can be used as the definitive guide for development and testing of the NewsPortal Flask web app.\n\n---\n\n=== app.py ===\nfrom flask import Flask, render_template, request, redirect, url_for\nimport os\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\napp = Flask(__name__)\n\nDATA_DIR = 'data'\n\n# Helper functions to read and write data files\n\ndef read_articles():\n    articles = []\n    try:\n        with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'articles.txt'), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n            for line in f:\n                line=line.strip()\n                if not line:\n                    continue\n                parts = line.split('|')\n                if len(parts) != 7:\n                    continue\n                article = {\n                    'article_id': parts[0],\n                    'title': parts[1],\n                    'author': parts[2],\n                    'category': parts[3],\n                    'content': parts[4],\n                    'date': parts[5],\n                    'views': int(parts[6])\n                }\n                articles.append(article)\n    except FileNotFoundError:\n        pass\n    return articles\n\n\ndef write_articles(articles):\n    with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'articles.txt'), 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n        for a in          # NewsPortal Flask Application Design Specification
         
         ## 1. Overview
         This document specifies the complete design of the NewsPortal Flask web app, covering all 9 pages with detailed element IDs, navigation flow starting from Dashboard, and local text file data storage formats.
         
         ---
         
         ## 2. Flask Page Templates and UI Elements
         
         ### 2.1 Dashboard Page
         - **Route:** `/dashboard` (Starting page)
         - **Page Title:** `News Portal`
         - **Container Div:** `id="dashboard-page"`
         - **UI Elements:**
           - `div` with `id="featured-articles"` - displays recommended featured articles
           - `button` with `id="browse-articles-button"` - navigates to Article Catalog page
           - `button` with `id="view-bookmarks-button"` - navigates to Bookmarks page
           - `button` with `id="trending-articles-button"` - navigates to Trending Articles page
         
         ### 2.2 Article Catalog Page
         - **Route:** `/catalog`
         - **Page Title:** `Article Catalog`
         - **Container Div:** `id="catalog-page"`
         - **UI Elements:**
           - `input` (text) with `id="search-input"` - to search articles by title, author, or keywords
           - `select` dropdown with `id="category-filter"` - categories filter (Technology, Sports, Business, Health, Entertainment, etc.)
           - `div` with `id="articles-grid"` - grid layout for article cards
           - For each article card:
              - `button` with `id="view-article-button-{article_id}"` - to view article details
         
         ### 2.3 Article Details Page
         - **Route:** `/article/<article_id>`
         - **Page Title:** `Article Details`
         - **Container Div:** `id="article-details-page"`
         - **UI Elements:**
           - `h1` with `id="article-title"` - article title
           - `div` with `id="article-author"` - article author
           - `div` with `id="article-date"` - publication date
           - `button` with `id="bookmark-button"` - to bookmark this article
           - `div` with `id="article-content"` - full article content
         
         ### 2.4 Bookmarks Page
         - **Route:** `/bookmarks`
         - **Page Title:** `My Bookmarks`
         - **Container Div:** `id="bookmarks-page"`
         - **UI Elements:**
           - `div` with `id="bookmarks-list"` - list showing bookmarked articles with title and date
           - For each bookmark:
             - `button` with `id="remove-bookmark-button-{bookmark_id}"` - remove bookmark
             - `button` with `id="read-bookmark-button-{bookmark_id}"` - read bookmarked article
           - `button` with `id="back-to-dashboard"` - navigate back to Dashboard
         
         ### 2.5 Comments Page
         - **Route:** `/comments`
         - **Page Title:** `Article Comments`
         - **Container Div:** `id="comments-page"`
         - **UI Elements:**
           - `div` with `id="comments-list"` - list of all comments with article title, commenter name, and comment text
           - `button` with `id="write-comment-button"` - navigate to Write Comment page
           - `select` dropdown with `id="filter-by-article"` - filter comments by article
           - `button` with `id="back-to-dashboard"` - navigate back to Dashboard
         
         ### 2.6 Write Comment Page
         - **Route:** `/write-comment`
         - **Page Title:** `Write a Comment`
         - **Container Div:** `id="write-comment-page"`
         - **UI Elements:**
           - `select` dropdown with `id="select-article"` - select article to comment on
           - `input` (text) with `id="commenter-name"` - enter commenter name
           - `textarea` with `id="comment-text"` - enter comment
           - `button` with `id="submit-comment-button"` - submit comment
         
         ### 2.7 Trending Articles Page
         - **Route:** `/trending`
         - **Page Title:** `Trending Articles`
         - **Container Div:** `id="trending-page"`
         - **UI Elements:**
           - `div` with `id="trending-list"` - ranked trending articles showing rank, title, category, view count
           - `select` dropdown with `id="time-period-filter"` - filter by time period (Today, This Week, This Month)
           - For each trending article:
             - `button` with `id="view-article-button-{article_id}"` - view article details
           - `button` with `id="back-to-dashboard"` - navigate back to Dashboard
         
         ### 2.8 Category Page
         - **Route:** `/category/<category_name>`
         - **Page Title:** `Category Articles`
         - **Container Div:** `id="category-page"`
         - **UI Elements:**
           - `h1` with `id="category-title"` - name of the category
           - `div` with `id="category-articles"` - list of articles in that category
           - `button` with `id="sort-by-date"` - sort articles by date
           - `button` with `id="sort-by-popularity"` - sort articles by popularity
           - `button` with `id="back-to-dashboard"` - navigate back to Dashboard
         
         ### 2.9 Search Results Page
         - **Route:** `/search-results`
         - **Page Title:** `Search Results`
         - **Container Div:** `id="search-results-page"`
         - **UI Elements:**
           - `div` with `id="search-query-display"` - display the executed search query
           - `div` with `id="results-list"` - list of articles matching the search
           - `div` with `id="no-results-message"` - message when no results found
           - `button` with `id="back-to-dashboard"` - navigate back to Dashboard
         
         ---
         
         ## 3. Navigation Flow
         
         - Application default start page: `/dashboard` (Dashboard Page)
         
         - From Dashboard:
           - `browse-articles-button` → `/catalog`
           - `view-bookmarks-button` → `/bookmarks`
           - `trending-articles-button` → `/trending`
         
         - From Article Catalog:
           - `view-article-button-{article_id}` → `/article/{article_id}`
           - Filter by category uses `/category/{category_name}` page
           - Search submits query and navigates to `/search-results`
           - No explicit back button (assumed via browser or nav bar)
         
         - From Article Details:
           - `bookmark-button` adds bookmark
           - Navigation back via browser or site nav (no explicit back button required)
         
         - From Bookmarks:
           - `remove-bookmark-button-{bookmark_id}` removes the bookmark
           - `read-bookmark-button-{bookmark_id}` navigates to `/article/{article_id}`
           - `back-to-dashboard` → `/dashboard`
         
         - From Comments:
           - `write-comment-button` → `/write-comment`
           - `filter-by-article` updates displayed comments
           - `back-to-dashboard` → `/dashboard`
         
         - From Write Comment:
           - `submit-comment-button` submits new comment and redirects to `/comments`
         
         - From Trending:
           - `view-article-button-{article_id}` → `/article/{article_id}`
           - `time-period-filter` changes trending articles display
           - `back-to-dashboard` → `/dashboard`
         
         - From Category:
           - `sort-by-date` sorts articles ascending/descending by date
           - `sort-by-popularity` sorts by views
           - `back-to-dashboard` → `/dashboard`
         
         - From Search Results:
           - `back-to-dashboard` → `/dashboard`
         
         ---
         
         ## 4. Local Text File Data Storage Formats and Usage
         
         All data is stored in the `data/` directory in UTF-8 encoded text files.
         
         ### 4.1 Articles Data (`articles.txt`)
         - **File Path:** `data/articles.txt`
         - **Format:** 
           ```
           article_id|title|author|category|content|date|views
           ```
         - **Example:**
           ```
           1|Breaking: New Technology Breakthrough|John Smith|Technology|Revolutionary advancement in quantum computing announced today|2025-01-20|5432
           2|Sports: Championship Victory|Sarah Johnson|Sports|Team wins the national championship with a thrilling final match|2025-01-19|3210
           3|Business: Market Trends Analysis|Michael Chen|Business|Expert analysis of current market conditions and forecasts|2025-01-18|2891
           ```
         - **Usage:** Load at app start or on-demand to display articles; update views on article reads.
         
         ### 4.2 Categories Data (`categories.txt`)
         - **File Path:** `data/categories.txt`
         - **Format:** 
           ```
           category_id|category_name|description
           ```
         - **Example:**
           ```
           1|Technology|Latest tech news and innovations
           2|Sports|Sports news and event coverage
           3|Business|Business and finance news
           ```
         - **Usage:** Populate category filters and category page displays.
         
         ### 4.3 Bookmarks Data (`bookmarks.txt`)
         - **File Path:** `data/bookmarks.txt`
         - **Format:**
           ```
           bookmark_id|article_id|article_title|bookmarked_date
           ```
         - **Example:**
           ```
           1|1|Breaking: New Technology Breakthrough|2025-01-20
           2|3|Business: Market Trends Analysis|2025-01-18
           ```
         - **Usage:** Read to show user bookmarks; add/remove bookmarks updates this file.
         
         ### 4.4 Comments Data (`comments.txt`)
         - **File Path:** `data/comments.txt`
         - **Format:**
           ```
           comment_id|article_id|article_title|commenter_name|comment_text|comment_date
           ```
         - **Example:**
           ```
           1|1|Breaking: New Technology Breakthrough|Alice Davis|Fascinating development!|2025-01-20
           2|2|Sports: Championship Victory|Robert Wilson|Amazing performance by the team!|2025-01-19
           ```
         - **Usage:** Read to display comments; append on new comment submission.
         
         ### 4.5 Trending Data (`trending.txt`)
         - **File Path:** `data/trending.txt`
         - **Format:**
           ```
           article_id|article_title|category|view_count|period
           ```
         - **Example:**
           ```
           1|Breaking: New Technology Breakthrough|Technology|5432|This Week
           2|Sports: Championship Victory|Sports|3210|This Week
           3|Business: Market Trends Analysis|Business|2891|This Month
           ```
         - **Usage:** Used for Trending page display filtered by time period.
         
         ---
         
         ## 5. Summary
         This design specification fully encompasses the required UI elements with exact IDs for all pages, the navigation flow starting from the Dashboard page, and the precise format and usage of all text file-based data stores as specified in the requirements.
         
         This spec can be used as the definitive guide for development and testing of the NewsPortal Flask web app.
         
         ---
         === user_task_description ===
         
         # Requirements Document for 'NewsPortal' Web Application
         
         ## 1. Objective
         Develop a comprehensive web application named 'NewsPortal' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse news articles by category, read detailed articles, bookmark favorites, view comments, and track trending articles. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.
         
         ## 2. Language
         The required development language for the 'NewsPortal' application is Python.
         
         ## 3. Page Design
         
         The 'NewsPortal' web application will consist of the following nine pages:
         
         ### 1. Dashboard Page
         - **Page Title**: News Portal
         - **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured articles, trending news, and quick navigation to all functionalities.
         - **Elements**:
           - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
           - **ID: featured-articles** - Type: Div - Display of featured article recommendations.
           - **ID: browse-articles-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to article catalog page.
           - **ID: view-bookmarks-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to bookmarks page.
           - **ID: trending-articles-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to trending articles page.
         
         ### 2. Article Catalog Page
         - **Page Title**: Article Catalog
         - **Overview**: A page displaying all available articles with search and filter capabilities.
         - **Elements**:
           - **ID: catalog-page** - Type: Div - Container for the catalog page.
           - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search articles by title, author, or keywords.
           - **ID: category-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by category (Technology, Sports, Business, Health, Entertainment, etc.).
           - **ID: articles-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying article cards with thumbnail, title, author, and date.
           - **ID: view-article-button-{article_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view article details (each article card has this).
         
         ### 3. Article Details Page
         - **Page Title**: Article Details
         - **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific article.
         - **Elements**:
           - **ID: article-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the article details page.
           - **ID: article-title** - Type: H1 - Display article title.
           - **ID: article-author** - Type: Div - Display article author.
           - **ID: article-date** - Type: Div - Display article publication date.
           - **ID: bookmark-button** - Type: Button - Button to bookmark the article.
           - **ID: article-content** - Type: Div - Section displaying the full article content.
         
         ### 4. Bookmarks Page
         - **Page Title**: My Bookmarks
         - **Overview**: A page displaying all bookmarked articles with removal and reading options.
         - **Elements**:
           - **ID: bookmarks-page** - Type: Div - Container for the bookmarks page.
           - **ID: bookmarks-list** - Type: Div - List displaying all bookmarked articles with title and date.
           - **ID: remove-bookmark-button-{bookmark_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove bookmark (each bookmark has this).
           - **ID: read-bookmark-button-{bookmark_id}** - Type: Button - Button to read bookmarked article (each bookmark has this).
           - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.
         
         ### 5. Comments Page
         - **Page Title**: Article Comments
         - **Overview**: A page displaying all comments on articles and allowing users to write new comments.
         - **Elements**:
           - **ID: comments-page** - Type: Div - Container for the comments page.
           - **ID: comments-list** - Type: Div - List of all comments with article title, commenter name, and comment text.
           - **ID: write-comment-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to write comment page.
           - **ID: filter-by-article** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter comments by article.
           - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.
         
         ### 6. Write Comment Page
         - **Page Title**: Write a Comment
         - **Overview**: A page for users to write comments on articles.
         - **Elements**:
           - **ID: write-comment-page** - Type: Div - Container for the write comment page.
           - **ID: select-article** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select article to comment on.
           - **ID: commenter-name** - Type: Input - Field to input commenter name.
           - **ID: comment-text** - Type: Textarea - Field to write comment text.
           - **ID: submit-comment-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit comment.
         
         ### 7. Trending Articles Page
         - **Page Title**: Trending Articles
         - **Overview**: A page displaying top trending articles ranked by views and engagement.
         - **Elements**:
           - **ID: trending-page** - Type: Div - Container for the trending articles page.
           - **ID: trending-list** - Type: Div - Ranked list of trending articles with rank, title, category, and view count.
           - **ID: time-period-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by time period (Today, This Week, This Month).
           - **ID: view-article-button-{article_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view article details (each trending article has this).
           - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.
         
         ### 8. Category Page
         - **Page Title**: Category Articles
         - **Overview**: A page displaying articles from a specific category.
         - **Elements**:
           - **ID: category-page** - Type: Div - Container for the category page.
           - **ID: category-title** - Type: H1 - Display the category name.
           - **ID: category-articles** - Type: Div - List of articles in the selected category.
           - **ID: sort-by-date** - Type: Button - Button to sort articles by date.
           - **ID: sort-by-popularity** - Type: Button - Button to sort articles by popularity.
           - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.
         
         ### 9. Search Results Page
         - **Page Title**: Search Results
         - **Overview**: A page displaying search results based on user query.
         - **Elements**:
           - **ID: search-results-page** - Type: Div - Container for the search results page.
           - **ID: search-query-display** - Type: Div - Display the search query performed.
           - **ID: results-list** - Type: Div - List of search results with article title and excerpt.
           - **ID: no-results-message** - Type: Div - Message displayed when no results found.
           - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.
         
         ## 4. Data Storage
         
         The 'NewsPortal' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:
         
         ### 1. Articles Data
         - **File Name**: `articles.txt`
         - **Data Format**:
           ```
           article_id|title|author|category|content|date|views
           ```
         - **Example Data**:
           ```
           1|Breaking: New Technology Breakthrough|John Smith|Technology|Revolutionary advancement in quantum computing announced today|2025-01-20|5432
           2|Sports: Championship Victory|Sarah Johnson|Sports|Team wins the national championship with a thrilling final match|2025-01-19|3210
           3|Business: Market Trends Analysis|Michael Chen|Business|Expert analysis of current market conditions and forecasts|2025-01-18|2891
           ```
         
         ### 2. Categories Data
         - **File Name**: `categories.txt`
         - **Data Format**:
           ```
           category_id|category_name|description
           ```
         - **Example Data**:
           ```
           1|Technology|Latest tech news and innovations
           2|Sports|Sports news and event coverage
           3|Business|Business and finance news
           ```
         
         ### 3. Bookmarks Data
         - **File Name**: `bookmarks.txt`
         - **Data Format**:
           ```
           bookmark_id|article_id|article_title|bookmarked_date
           ```
         - **Example Data**:
           ```
           1|1|Breaking: New Technology Breakthrough|2025-01-20
           2|3|Business: Market Trends Analysis|2025-01-18
           ```
         
         ### 4. Comments Data
         - **File Name**: `comments.txt`
         - **Data Format**:
           ```
           comment_id|article_id|article_title|commenter_name|comment_text|comment_date
           ```
         - **Example Data**:
           ```
           1|1|Breaking: New Technology Breakthrough|Alice Davis|Fascinating development!|2025-01-20
           2|2|Sports: Championship Victory|Robert Wilson|Amazing performance by the team!|2025-01-19
           ```
         
         ### 5. Trending Data
         - **File Name**: `trending.txt`
         - **Data Format**:
           ```
           article_id|article_title|category|view_count|period
           ```
         - **Example Data**:
           ```
           1|Breaking: New Technology Breakthrough|Technology|5432|This Week
           2|Sports: Championship Victory|Sports|3210|This Week
           3|Business: Market Trends Analysis|Business|2891|This Month
           ```
         
         
         === design_spec.md ===
         # NewsPortal Flask Application Design Specification
         
         ## 1. Overview
         This document specifies the complete design of the NewsPortal Flask web app, covering all 9 pages with detailed element IDs, navigation flow starting from Dashboard, and local text file data storage formats.
         
         ---
         
         ## 2. Flask Page Templates and UI Elements
         
         ### 2.1 Dashboard Page
         - **Route:** `/dashboard` (Starting page)
         - **Page Title:** `News Portal`
         - **Container Div:** `id="dashboard-page"`
         - **UI Elements:**
           - `div` with `id="featured-articles"` - displays recommended featured articles
           - `button` with `id="browse-articles-button"` - navigates to Article Catalog page
           - `button` with `id="view-bookmarks-button"` - navigates to Bookmarks page
           - `button` with `id="trending-articles-button"` - navigates to Trending Articles page
         
         ### 2.2 Article Catalog Page
         - **Route:** `/catalog`
         - **Page Title:** `Article Catalog`
         - **Container Div:** `id="catalog-page"`
         - **UI Elements:**
           - `input` (text) with `id="search-input"` - to search articles by title, author, or keywords
           - `select` dropdown with `id="category-filter"` - categories filter (Technology, Sports, Business, Health, Entertainment, etc.)
           - `div` with `id="articles-grid"` - grid layout for article cards
           - For each article card:
              - `button` with `id="view-article-button-{article_id}"` - to view article details
         
         ### 2.3 Article Details Page
         - **Route:** `/article/<article_id>`
         - **Page Title:** `Article Details`
         - **Container Div:** `id="article-details-page"`
         - **UI Elements:**
           - `h1` with `id="article-title"` - article title
           - `div` with `id="article-author"` - article author
           - `div` with `id="article-date"` - publication date
           - `button` with `id="bookmark-button"` - to bookmark this article
           - `div` with `id="article-content"` - full article content
         
         ### 2.4 Bookmarks Page
         - **Route:** `/bookmarks`
         - **Page Title:** `My Bookmarks`
         - **Container Div:** `id="bookmarks-page"`
         - **UI Elements:**
           - `div` with `id="bookmarks-list"` - list showing bookmarked articles with title and date
           - For each bookmark:
             - `button` with `id="remove-bookmark-button-{bookmark_id}"` - remove bookmark
             - `button` with `id="read-bookmark-button-{bookmark_id}"` - read bookmarked article
           - `button` with `id="back-to-dashboard"` - navigate back to Dashboard
         
         ### 2.5 Comments Page
         - **Route:** `/comments`
         - **Page Title:** `Article Comments`
         - **Container Div:** `id="comments-page"`
         - **UI Elements:**
           - `div` with `id="comments-list"` - list of all comments with article title, commenter name, and comment text
           - `button` with `id="write-comment-button"` - navigate to Write Comment page
           - `select` dropdown with `id="filter-by-article"` - filter comments by article
           - `button` with `id="back-to-dashboard"` - navigate back to Dashboard
         
         ### 2.6 Write Comment Page
         - **Route:** `/write-comment`
         - **Page Title:** `Write a Comment`
         - **Container Div:** `id="write-comment-page"`
         - **UI Elements:**
           - `select` dropdown with `id="select-article"` - select article to comment on
           - `input` (text) with `id="commenter-name"` - enter commenter name
           - `textarea` with `id="comment-text"` - enter comment
           - `button` with `id="submit-comment-button"` - submit comment
         
         ### 2.7 Trending Articles Page
         - **Route:** `/trending`
         - **Page Title:** `Trending Articles`
         - **Container Div:** `id="trending-page"`
         - **UI Elements:**
           - `div` with `id="trending-list"` - ranked trending articles showing rank, title, category, view count
           - `select` dropdown with `id="time-period-filter"` - filter by time period (Today, This Week, This Month)
           - For each trending article:
             - `button` with `id="view-article-button-{article_id}"` - view article details
           - `button` with `id="back-to-dashboard"` - navigate back to Dashboard
         
         ### 2.8 Category Page
         - **Route:** `/category/<category_name>`
         - **Page Title:** `Category Articles`
         - **Container Div:** `id="category-page"`
         - **UI Elements:**
           - `h1` with `id="category-title"` - name of the category
           - `div` with `id="category-articles"` - list of articles in that category
           - `button` with `id="sort-by-date"` - sort articles by date
           - `button` with `id="sort-by-popularity"` - sort articles by popularity
           - `button` with `id="back-to-dashboard"` - navigate back to Dashboard
         
         ### 2.9 Search Results Page
         - **Route:** `/search-results`
         - **Page Title:** `Search Results`
         - **Container Div:** `id="search-results-page"`
         - **UI Elements:**
           - `div` with `id="search-query-display"` - display the executed search query
           - `div` with `id="results-list"` - list of articles matching the search
           - `div` with `id="no-results-message"` - message when no results found
           - `button` with `id="back-to-dashboard"` - navigate back to Dashboard
         
         ---
         
         ## 3. Navigation Flow
         
         - Application default start page: `/dashboard` (Dashboard Page)
         
         - From Dashboard:
           - `browse-articles-button` → `/catalog`
           - `view-bookmarks-button` → `/bookmarks`
           - `trending-articles-button` → `/trending`
         
         - From Article Catalog:
           - `view-article-button-{article_id}` → `/article/{article_id}`
           - Filter by category uses `/category/{category_name}` page
           - Search submits query and navigates to `/search-results`
           - No explicit back button (assumed via browser or nav bar)
         
         - From Article Details:
           - `bookmark-button` adds bookmark
           - Navigation back via browser or site nav (no explicit back button required)
         
         - From Bookmarks:
           - `remove-bookmark-button-{bookmark_id}` removes the bookmark
           - `read-bookmark-button-{bookmark_id}` navigates to `/article/{article_id}`
           - `back-to-dashboard` → `/dashboard`
         
         - From Comments:
           - `write-comment-button` → `/write-comment`
           - `filter-by-article` updates displayed comments
           - `back-to-dashboard` → `/dashboard`
         
         - From Write Comment:
           - `submit-comment-button` submits new comment and redirects to `/comments`
         
         - From Trending:
           - `view-article-button-{article_id}` → `/article/{article_id}`
           - `time-period-filter` changes trending articles display
           - `back-to-dashboard` → `/dashboard`
         
         - From Category:
           - `sort-by-date` sorts articles ascending/descending by date
           - `sort-by-popularity` sorts by views
           - `back-to-dashboard` → `/dashboard`
         
         - From Search Results:
           - `back-to-dashboard` → `/dashboard`
         
         ---
         
         ## 4. Local Text File Data Storage Formats and Usage
         
         All data is stored in the `data/` directory in UTF-8 encoded text files.
         
         ### 4.1 Articles Data (`articles.txt`)
         - **File Path:** `data/articles.txt`
         - **Format:** 
           ```
           article_id|title|author|category|content|date|views
           ```
         - **Example:**
           ```
           1|Breaking: New Technology Breakthrough|John Smith|Technology|Revolutionary advancement in quantum computing announced today|2025-01-20|5432
           2|Sports: Championship Victory|Sarah Johnson|Sports|Team wins the national championship with a thrilling final match|2025-01-19|3210
           3|Business: Market Trends Analysis|Michael Chen|Business|Expert analysis of current market conditions and forecasts|2025-01-18|2891
           ```
         - **Usage:** Load at app start or on-demand to display articles; update views on article reads.
         
         ### 4.2 Categories Data (`categories.txt`)
         - **File Path:** `data/categories.txt`
         - **Format:** 
           ```
           category_id|category_name|description
           ```
         - **Example:**
           ```
           1|Technology|Latest tech news and innovations
           2|Sports|Sports news and event coverage
           3|Business|Business and finance news
           ```
         - **Usage:** Populate category filters and category page displays.
         
         ### 4.3 Bookmarks Data (`bookmarks.txt`)
         - **File Path:** `data/bookmarks.txt`
         - **Format:**
           ```
           bookmark_id|article_id|article_title|bookmarked_date
           ```
         - **Example:**
           ```
           1|1|Breaking: New Technology Breakthrough|2025-01-20
           2|3|Business: Market Trends Analysis|2025-01-18
           ```
         - **Usage:** Read to show user bookmarks; add/remove bookmarks updates this file.
         
         ### 4.4 Comments Data (`comments.txt`)
         - **File Path:** `data/comments.txt`
         - **Format:**
           ```
           comment_id|article_id|article_title|commenter_name|comment_text|comment_date
           ```
         - **Example:**
           ```
           1|1|Breaking: New Technology Breakthrough|Alice Davis|Fascinating development!|2025-01-20
           2|2|Sports: Championship Victory|Robert Wilson|Amazing performance by the team!|2025-01-19
           ```
         - **Usage:** Read to display comments; append on new comment submission.
         
         ### 4.5 Trending Data (`trending.txt`)
         - **File Path:** `data/trending.txt`
         - **Format:**
           ```
           article_id|article_title|category|view_count|period
           ```
         - **Example:**
           ```
           1|Breaking: New Technology Breakthrough|Technology|5432|This Week
           2|Sports: Championship Victory|Sports|3210|This Week
           3|Business: Market Trends Analysis|Business|2891|This Month
           ```
         - **Usage:** Used for Trending page display filtered by time period.
         
         ---
         
         ## 5. Summary
         This design specification fully encompasses the required UI elements with exact IDs for all pages, the navigation flow starting from the Dashboard page, and the precise format and usage of all text file-based data stores as specified in the requirements.
         
         This spec can be used as the definitive guide for development and testing of the NewsPortal Flask web app.
